Grand Prix Trial Winners
========================



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX DALLAS/FORT WORTH 2015](/en/events/coverage/gpdal15)
 on July 25, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/calderaro.jpg)
By Marc Calderaro











Though it's been hot in Texas for a long time, the summer of *Magic Origins* has just begun. Here are all the players who've proved themselves in *Magic Origins* Sealed enough to earn two byes going into Grand Prix Dallas/Fort Worth.







#### Jonathan Hubbard – Grand Prix Trial Winner


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-4e32206a5c616252bc4a226230dc78e4?n=Jonathan%20Hubbard%20%E2%80%93%20Grand%20Prix%20Trial%20Winner)

[통계](#none)
[표본 손](#none)

개요색비용희귀도
